</ul></div><article class="seo-footer_seo-footer__0QQFN"><div class="seo-footer_seo-footer__headline__hHO0a">Clothing</div><div class="seo-footer_seo-footer__description__BH0ZA"><h2>The infinite universe of women's clothing.</h2>
<p>Little black dresses, long floral skirts, skinny trousers... dressy here, casual there, women's clothes are chosen to match the occasion. From basics that go with everything to sophisticated pieces that tell the whole story, a women's wardrobe is all that and more.</p>
<p>The category of women's clothing includes short-sleeved tops, long-sleeves tops, <a href="/women-clothing/skirts/">skirts of all shapes and sizes</a> and trousers and jeans. To protect us against the elements, it also includes jackets, overcoats, blousons and trench coats. Finally, it includes lingerie and beach and swimwear. Here, you will find every material under the sun, from wool to cashmere, leather to fur, linen to cotton, with a large section devoted to denim. Clothes for women come in a vast palette of single-colour tones or adorned with bold decoration like spotty patterns, houndstooth check, plant and animal prints.</p>
<p>The clothes in this category are from the collections of a wide array of French and international brands. The highly-respected fashion houses, like <a href="/women-clothing/chanel/">Chanel</a> and Yves Saint Laurent, are sharing the billing with more recent labels like Tory Burch, Tara Jarmon and Marni, but they are also joined by the new designers in vogue. Women will be won over by designer pieces, like this Courrèges A-line dress or this <a href="/women-clothing/dresses/isabel-marant/silk/">silk dress by Isabel Marant</a>, or opt for basics, which will enhance any outfit.</p></div></article></div></div></div></div></main><div class="bottom-navigation_bottomNavigation__EtCMs"><a href="/" class="bottom-navigation_bottomNavigation__button__M8rp_"
